   <p class="normal">2.Â Â Â Where personal data are transferred to a third country or to an international organisation, the data subject shall have the right to be informed of the appropriate safeguards pursuant to Article 46 relating to the transfer.</p>
   <p class="normal">3.Â Â Â The controller shall provide a copy of the personal data undergoing processing. For any further copies requested by the data subject, the controller may charge a reasonable fee based on administrative costs. Where the data subject makes the request by electronic means, and unless otherwise requested by the data subject, the information shall be provided in a commonly used electronic form.</p>
   <p class="normal">4.Â Â Â The right to obtain a copy referred to in paragraph 3 shall not adversely affect the rights and freedoms of others.</p>
   <p id="d1e2589-1-1" class="ti-section-1">
      <span class="expanded">Section 3</span>
   </p>
   <p id="L_2016119EN.01000101-d-006" class="ti-section-2">
      <span class="bold">
         <span class="expanded">Rectification and erasure</span>
      </span>
   </p>
   <p id="d1e2599-1-1" class="ti-art">Article 16</p>
   <p class="sti-art">Right to rectification</p>
   <p class="normal">The data subject shall have the right to obtain from the controller without undue delay the rectification of inaccurate personal data concerning him or her. Taking into account the purposes of the processing, the data subject shall have the right to have incomplete personal data completed, including by means of providing a supplementary statement.</p>
   <p id="d1e2606-1-1" class="ti-art">Article 17</p>
   <p class="sti-art">Right to erasure (â€˜right to be forgottenâ€™)</p>
   <p class="normal">1.Â Â Â The data subject shall have the right to obtain from the controller the erasure of personal data concerning him or her without undue delay and the controller shall have the obligation to erase personal data without undue delay where one of the following grounds applies:</p>
   <table width="100%" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
      <col width="4%"/>
      <col width="96%"/>
      <tbody>
         <tr>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">(a)</p>
            </td>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">the personal data are no longer necessary in relation to the purposes for which they were collected or otherwise processed;</p>
            </td>
         </tr>
      </tbody>
   </table>
   <table width="100%" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
      <col width="4%"/>
      <col width="96%"/>
      <tbody>
         <tr>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">(b)</p>
            </td>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">the data subject withdraws consent on which the processing is based according to pointÂ (a) of Article 6(1), or pointÂ (a) of Article 9(2), and where there is no other legal ground for the processing;</p>
            </td>
         </tr>
      </tbody>
   </table>
   <table width="100%" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
      <col width="4%"/>
      <col width="96%"/>
      <tbody>
         <tr>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">(c)</p>
            </td>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">the data subject objects to the processing pursuant to Article 21(1) and there are no overriding legitimate grounds for the processing, or the data subject objects to the processing pursuant to Article 21(2);</p>
            </td>
         </tr>
      </tbody>
   </table>
   <table width="100%" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
      <col width="4%"/>
      <col width="96%"/>
      <tbody>
         <tr>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">(d)</p>
            </td>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">the personal data have been unlawfully processed;</p>
            </td>
         </tr>
      </tbody>
   </table>
   <table width="100%" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
      <col width="4%"/>
      <col width="96%"/>
      <tbody>
         <tr>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">(e)</p>
            </td>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">the personal data have to be erased for compliance with a legal obligation in Union or MemberÂ State law to which the controller is subject;</p>
            </td>
         </tr>
      </tbody>
   </table>
   <table width="100%" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
      <col width="4%"/>
      <col width="96%"/>
      <tbody>
         <tr>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">(f)</p>
            </td>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">the personal data have been collected in relation to the offer of information society services referred to in ArticleÂ 8(1).</p>
            </td>
         </tr>
      </tbody>
   </table>
   <p class="normal">2.Â Â Â Where the controller has made the personal data public and is obliged pursuant to paragraphÂ 1 to erase the personal data, the controller, taking account of available technology and the cost of implementation, shall take reasonable steps, including technical measures, to inform controllers which are processing the personal data that the data subject has requested the erasure by such controllers of any links to, or copy or replication of, those personal data.</p>
   <p class="normal">3.Â Â Â Paragraphs 1 and 2 shall not apply to the extent that processing is necessary:</p>
   <table width="100%" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
      <col width="4%"/>
      <col width="96%"/>
      <tbody>
         <tr>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">(a)</p>
            </td>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">for exercising the right of freedom of expression and information;</p>
            </td>
         </tr>
      </tbody>
   </table>
   <table width="100%" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
      <col width="4%"/>
      <col width="96%"/>
      <tbody>
         <tr>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">(b)</p>
            </td>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">for compliance with a legal obligation which requires processing by Union or MemberÂ State law to which the controller is subject or for the performance of a task carried out in the public interest or in the exercise of official authority vested in the controller;</p>
            </td>
         </tr>
      </tbody>
   </table>
   <table width="100%" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
      <col width="4%"/>
      <col width="96%"/>
      <tbody>
         <tr>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">(c)</p>
            </td>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">for reasons of public interest in the area of public health in accordance with pointsÂ (h) and (i) of Article 9(2) as well as Article 9(3);</p>
            </td>
         </tr>
      </tbody>
   </table>
   <table width="100%" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
      <col width="4%"/>
      <col width="96%"/>
      <tbody>
         <tr>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">(d)</p>
            </td>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">for archiving purposes in the public interest, scientific or historical research purposes or statistical purposes in accordance with Article 89(1) in so far as the right referred to in paragraphÂ 1 is likely to render impossible or seriously impair the achievement of the objectives of that processing; or</p>
            </td>
         </tr>
      </tbody>
   </table>
   <table width="100%" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
      <col width="4%"/>
      <col width="96%"/>
      <tbody>
         <tr>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">(e)</p>
            </td>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">for the establishment, exercise or defence of legal claims.</p>
            </td>
         </tr>
      </tbody>
   </table>
   <p id="d1e2700-1-1" class="ti-art">Article 18</p>
   <p class="sti-art">Right to restriction of processing</p>
   <p class="normal">1.Â Â Â The data subject shall have the right to obtain from the controller restriction of processing where one of the following applies:</p>
   <table width="100%" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
      <col width="4%"/>
      <col width="96%"/>
      <tbody>
         <tr>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">(a)</p>
            </td>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">the accuracy of the personal data is contested by the data subject, for a period enabling the controller to verify the accuracy of the personal data;</p>
            </td>
         </tr>
      </tbody>
   </table>
   <table width="100%" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
      <col width="4%"/>
      <col width="96%"/>
      <tbody>
         <tr>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">(b)</p>
            </td>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">the processing is unlawful and the data subject opposes the erasure of the personal data and requests the restriction of their use instead;</p>
            </td>
         </tr>
      </tbody>
   </table>
   <table width="100%" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
      <col width="4%"/>
      <col width="96%"/>
      <tbody>
         <tr>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">(c)</p>
            </td>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">the controller no longer needs the personal data for the purposes of the processing, but they are required by the data subject for the establishment, exercise or defence of legal claims;</p>
            </td>
         </tr>
      </tbody>
   </table>
   <table width="100%" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
      <col width="4%"/>
      <col width="96%"/>
      <tbody>
         <tr>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">(d)</p>
            </td>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">the data subject has objected to processing pursuant to ArticleÂ 21(1) pending the verification whether the legitimate grounds of the controller override those of the data subject.</p>
            </td>
         </tr>
      </tbody>
   </table>
   <p class="normal">2.Â Â Â Where processing has been restricted under paragraph 1, such personal data shall, with the exception of storage, only be processed with the data subject's consent or for the establishment, exercise or defence of legal claims or for the protection of the rights of another natural or legal person or for reasons of important public interest of the Union or of a MemberÂ State.</p>
   <p class="normal">3.Â Â Â A data subject who has obtained restriction of processing pursuant to paragraphÂ 1 shall be informed by the controller before the restriction of processing is lifted.</p>
   <p id="d1e2746-1-1" class="ti-art">Article 19</p>
   <p class="sti-art">Notification obligation regarding rectification or erasure of personal data or restriction of processing</p>
   <p class="normal">The controller shall communicate any rectification or erasure of personal data or restriction of processing carried out in accordance with ArticleÂ 16, Article 17(1) and Article 18 to each recipient to whom the personal data have been disclosed, unless this proves impossible or involves disproportionate effort. The controller shall inform the data subject about those recipients if the data subject requests it.</p>
   <p id="d1e2753-1-1" class="ti-art">Article 20</p>
   <p class="sti-art">Right to data portability</p>
   <p class="normal">1.Â Â Â The data subject shall have the right to receive the personal data concerning him or her, which he or she has provided to a controller, in a structured, commonly used and machine-readable format and have the right to transmit those data to another controller without hindrance from the controller to which the personal data have been provided, where:</p>
   <table width="100%" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
      <col width="4%"/>
      <col width="96%"/>
      <tbody>
         <tr>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">(a)</p>
            </td>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">the processing is based on consent pursuant to point (a) of Article 6(1) or pointÂ (a) of Article 9(2) or on a contract pursuant to point (b) of Article 6(1); and</p>
            </td>
         </tr>
      </tbody>
   </table>
   <table width="100%" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
      <col width="4%"/>
      <col width="96%"/>
      <tbody>
         <tr>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">(b)</p>
            </td>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">the processing is carried out by automated means.</p>
            </td>
         </tr>
      </tbody>
   </table>
   <p class="normal">2.Â Â Â In exercising his or her right to data portability pursuant to paragraph 1, the data subject shall have the right to have the personal data transmitted directly from one controller to another, where technically feasible.</p>
   <p class="normal">3.Â Â Â The exercise of the right referred to in paragraphÂ 1 of this Article shall be without prejudice to ArticleÂ 17. That right shall not apply to processing necessary for the performance of a task carried out in the public interest or in the exercise of official authority vested in the controller.</p>
   <p class="normal">4.Â Â Â The right referred to in paragraphÂ 1 shall not adversely affect the rights and freedoms of others.</p>
   <p id="d1e2793-1-1" class="ti-section-1">
      <span class="expanded">Section 4</span>
   </p>
   <p id="L_2016119EN.01000101-d-007" class="ti-section-2">
      <span class="bold">
         <span class="expanded">Right to object and automated individual decision-making</span>
      </span>
   </p>
   <p id="d1e2803-1-1" class="ti-art">Article 21</p>
   <p class="sti-art">Right to object</p>
   <p class="normal">1.Â Â Â The data subject shall have the right to object, on grounds relating to his or her particular situation, at any time to processing of personal data concerning him or her which is based on point (e) or (f) of Article 6(1), including profiling based on those provisions. The controller shall no longer process the personal data unless the controller demonstrates compelling legitimate grounds for the processing which override the interests, rights and freedoms of the data subject or for the establishment, exercise or defence of legal claims.</p>
   <p class="normal">2.Â Â Â Where personal data are processed for direct marketing purposes, the data subject shall have the right to object at any time to processing of personal data concerning him or her for such marketing, which includes profiling to the extent that it is related to such direct marketing.</p>
   <p class="normal">3.Â Â Â Where the data subject objects to processing for direct marketing purposes, the personal data shall no longer be processed for such purposes.</p>
   <p class="normal">4.Â Â Â At the latest at the time of the first communication with the data subject, the right referred to in paragraphsÂ 1 and 2 shall be explicitly brought to the attention of the data subject and shall be presented clearly and separately from any other information.</p>
   <p class="normal">5.Â Â Â In the context of the use of information society services, and notwithstanding DirectiveÂ 2002/58/EC, the data subject may exercise his or her right to object by automated means using technical specifications.</p>
   <p class="normal">6.Â Â Â Where personal data are processed for scientific or historical research purposes or statistical purposes pursuant to ArticleÂ 89(1), the data subject, on grounds relating to his or her particular situation, shall have the right to object to processing of personal data concerning him or her, unless the processing is necessary for the performance of a task carried out for reasons of public interest.</p>
   <p id="d1e2838-1-1" class="ti-art">Article 22</p>
   <p class="sti-art">Automated individual decision-making, including profiling</p>
   <p class="normal">1.Â Â Â The data subject shall have the right not to be subject to a decision based solely on automated processing, including profiling, which produces legal effects concerning him or her or similarly significantly affects him or her.</p>
   <p class="normal">2.Â Â Â ParagraphÂ 1 shall not apply if the decision:</p>
   <table width="100%" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
      <col width="4%"/>
      <col width="96%"/>
      <tbody>
         <tr>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">(a)</p>
            </td>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">is necessary for entering into, or performance of, a contract between the data subject and a data controller;</p>
            </td>
         </tr>
      </tbody>
   </table>
   <table width="100%" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
      <col width="4%"/>
      <col width="96%"/>
      <tbody>
         <tr>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">(b)</p>
            </td>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">is authorised by Union or MemberÂ State law to which the controller is subject and which also lays down suitable measures to safeguard the data subject's rights and freedoms and legitimate interests; or</p>
            </td>
         </tr>
      </tbody>
   </table>
   <table width="100%" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
      <col width="4%"/>
      <col width="96%"/>
      <tbody>
         <tr>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">(c)</p>
            </td>
            <td valign="top">
               <p class="normal">is based on the data subject's explicit consent.</p>
            </td>
         </tr>
      </tbody>
   </table>
   <p class="normal">3.Â Â Â In the cases referred to in points (a) and (c) of paragraphÂ 2, the data controller shall implement suitable measures to safeguard the data subject's rights and freedoms and legitimate interests, at least the right to obtain human intervention on the part of the controller, to express his or her point of view and to contest the decision.</p>
   <p class="normal">4.Â Â Â Decisions referred to in paragraph 2 shall not be based on special categories of personal data referred to in ArticleÂ 9(1), unless point (a) or (g) of Article 9(2) applies and suitable measures to safeguard the data subject's rights and freedoms and legitimate interests are in place.</p>
   <p id="d1e2884-1-1" class="ti-section-1">
      <span class="expanded">Section 5</span>
   </p>

      <span class="bold">
         <span class="expanded">Restrictions</span>

   <p id="d1e2894-1-1" class="ti-art">Article 23</p>
   <p class="sti-art">Restrictions</p>
   <p class="normal">1.Â Â Â Union or MemberÂ State law to which the data controller or processor is subject may restrict by way of a legislative measure the scope of the obligations and rights provided for in ArticlesÂ 12 to 22 and ArticleÂ 34, as well as ArticleÂ 5 in so far as its provisions correspond to the rights and obligations provided for in ArticlesÂ 12 to 22, when such a restriction respects the essence of the fundamental rights and freedoms and is a necessary and proportionate measure in a democratic society to safeguard:</p>
